*/\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\nimport { useVoice } from '../../hooks/useVoice';\n\ninterface AgenticBarProps {\n    variant?: 'floating' | 'inline' | 'minimal' true,\n    showWaveform = true,\n    onCommand,\n    className = ''\n}: AgenticBarProps) {\n    const [lastResponse, setLastResponse] = useState('');\n    const [pulseIntensity, setPulseIntensity] =    stop,\n        toggle\n    } = useVoice({\n        userType,\n        onTranscript: (text, isFinal) => {\n            if (!isFinal) {\n                // Animate based on speech\n                setPulseIntensity(Math.min(text.length / 10, 1));\n            }\n        },\n        onResponse: (data) => {\n            const text = data?.response?.text || data?.tts_response?.text || '';\n            setLastResponse(text);\n            onCommand?.(transcript, data);\n        },\n        onStateChange: (newState) => {\n            if (newState === 'listening') {\n                setPulseIntensity(0.5);\n            } else if (newState === 'idle') {\n                setPulseIntensity(0);\n            }\n        }\n    });\n    \n    // Position styles\n    const positionStyles: Record<string, string> = {\n        'bottom': 'bottom-6 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2',\n        'top': 'top-6 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2',\n        'bottom-right': 'bottom-6 right-6',\n        'bottom-left': 'bottom-6 left-6'\n    };\n    \n    // State colors with gradients\n    const stateStyles: Record<string, { bg: string; glow: string; icon: string }> = {\n        idle: {\n glow: 'shadow-lg shadow-red-500/50',\n            icon: '\u274c'\n        }\n    };\n    \n    const currentStyle = stateStyles[state] || stateStyles.idle;\n    \n    // Minimal variant - just a z-50\n                    w-14 h-14 rounded-full\n                    ${currentStyle.bg} ${currentStyle.glow}\n                    text-white text-2xl\n                    flex items-center justify-center\n                    transition-all duration-300 transform hover:scale-110\n                    border-2 border-white/20\n                    ${className}\n                `}\n                title={isListening ? 'Click to stop' : 'Click to speak'}\n            >\n                {currentStyle.icon}\n            </button>\n        );\n    }\n    \n    // Walker variant - follows cursor\n    if (variant === 'walker') {\n        return (\n            <div className={`fixed ${positionStyles[position]} z-50 ${className}`}>\n                <div className={`\n                    flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2 rounded-full\n                    ${currentStyle.bg} ${currentStyle.glow}\n                    border border-white/10 backdrop-blur-sm\n                    transition-all duration-300\n                `}>\n                    <button\n                        onClick={toggle}\n                        className=\"w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-white/20 flex items-center justify-center text-xl hover:bg-white/30 transition-all\"\n                    >\n                        {currentStyle.icon}\n                    </button>\n                    \n                    {(interimTranscript || </span>\n                    )}\n                    \n                    {isListening && showWaveform && (\n                        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-0.5\">\n                            {[...Array(5)].map((_, i) => (\n                                <div\n                                    key={i}\n                                    className=\"w-1 bg-white rounded-full </div>\n            </div>\n        );\n    }\n    \n    // Inline variant\n    if (variant === 'inline') {\n        return (\n            <div className={`flex items-center gap-3 ${className}`}>\n `}\n                >\n                    {currentStyle.icon}\n                </button>\n                \n                {showTranscript && (interimTranscript || transcript || lastResponse) && (\n truncate\">{interimTranscript}</p>\n                        )}\n                        {transcript && !interimTranscript && (\n                            <p className=\"text-white text-sm border border-white/10 shadow-2xl\n                p-4 min-w-[320px] max-w-[400px]\n                transition-all duration-300\n                ${isListening ? */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\nimport { useVoice } from '../hooks/useVoice';\n\ninterface WalkingCursorProps {\n    enabled?: boolean;\n    showVoice?: setIsVisible] = useState(true);\n    const targetRef = useRef({ x: 100, y: 100 });\n    const animationRef = useRef<number>();\n    \n    const { state, transcript, interimTranscript, isListening, toggle } = useVoice({\n        userType: 'boss',\n        onResponse: (data) => {\n            console.log('[Walker] Got response:', data);\n        }\n    });\n    \n    // Follow mouse smoothly\n    useEffect(() => {\n        if (!enabled) return;\n        \n        const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {\n            targetRef.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };\n        };\n        \n        window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);\n        \n        const animate = () => {\n            setPosition(prev => ({\n                x: prev.x + (targetRef.current.x - prev.x) * 0.1,\n                y: prev.y + (targetRef.current.y - prev.y) * 0.1\n            }));\n            animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n        };\n        \n        animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n        \n        return () => {\n            window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);\n            if (animationRef.current) cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);\n        };\n    }, [enabled]);\n    \n    if (!enabled || !isVisible) return null;\n    \n    return (\n        <div\n            className=\"fixed pointer-events-none z-[9999] transition-opacity duration-300\"\n            style={{\n                left: position.x + 20,\n                top: position.y + 20,\n                transform: 'translate(0, 0)'\n            }}\n        >\n            <div className={`\n                flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-full\n                ${isListening \n                    ? '\ud83c\udfa4' : '\ud83c\udf99\ufe0f'}\n                </span>\n                \n                {/* Status/transcript */}\n                {showVoice && (\n                    <span className=\"text-white text-xs max-w-[150px] truncate\">\n                        {interimTranscript || transcript || (isListening ? 'SIGNINVOICE'\n/**\n * Re-exports for backward compatibility\n */\n\n// Voice hook from main location\nexport { useVoice, default } from '../../../hooks/useVoice';\n\n// Utility functions\nexport function formatPhoneNumber(phone: string): string {\n    if (!phone) return '';\n    const cleaned = phone.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    if (cleaned.length === 10) {\n        return `(${cleaned.slice(0, 3)}) ${cleaned.slice(3, 6)}-${cleaned.slice(6)}`;\n    }\n    return phone;\n}\n\nexport function speakablePhone(phone: string): string {\n    return phone.replace(/\\D/g, '').split('').join(' ');\n}\n\nexport function validatePhoneNumber(phone: string): boolean {\n    return phone.replace(/\\D/g, '').length >= 10;\n}\n\nexport function validateEmail(email: string): boolean {\n    return }).format(amount);\n}\n\nexport function debounce<T extends (...args: any[]) => any>(func: T, wait: number) {\n    let timeout: NodeJS.Timeout;\n    return (...args: Parameters<T>) => {\n        clearTimeout(timeout);\n        timeout = setTimeout(() => func(...args), wait);\n    };\n}\n\nexport function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {\n    return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n                const t = event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) final += t;\\n                else interim += t;\\n            }\\n            \\n            setInterimTranscript(interim);\\n            optionsRef.current.onTranscript?.(interim, false);\\n            \\n            if (final.trim()) {\\n                console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udcdd Got:', final.trim());\\n                setTranscript(final.trim());\\n                optionsRef.current.onTranscript?.(final.trim(), true);\\n                processVoiceInput(final.trim());\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        globalRecognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') return;\\n            console.error('[Voice] \\u274c', event.error);\\n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n                setError('Microphone access denied');\\n                setState('error');\\n                shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        globalRecognition.onend = () => {\\n            globalIsActive = false;\\n            if (shouldRunRef.current && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\\n                if (restartTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\\n                restartTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {\\n                    if (shouldRunRef.current && !globalIsActive && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\\n                        safeStart();\\n                    }\\n                }, 1000);\\n            } else {\\n                setState('idle');\\n                optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('idle');\\n            }\\n        };\\n    }, [processVoiceInput, safeStart]);\\n    \\n    const start = useCallback(() => {\\n        console.log('[Voice] \\u25b6\\ufe0f START');\\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n        shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n        setError(null);\\n        setState('listening');\\n        safeStart();\\n    }, [safeStart]);\\n    \\n    const stop = useCallback(() => {\\n        console.log('[Voice] \\u23f9\\ufe0f STOP');\\n        shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n        if (restartTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(restartTimeoutRef.current);\\n        if (globalRecognition && globalIsActive) {\\n            try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\\n        }\\n        setState('idle');\\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('idle');\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    const toggle = useCallback(() => {\\n        shouldRunRef.current || state === 'listening' ? stop() : start();\\n    }, [state, start, stop]);\\n    \\n    const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n        if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n        console.log('[Voice] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text);\\n        \\n        const wasRunning = shouldRunRef.current;\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = true;\\n        \\n        if (globalIsActive && globalRecognition) {\\n            try { globalRecognition.stop(); } catch {}\\n        }\\n        \\n        synthRef.current.cancel();\\n        setState('speaking');\\n        optionsRef.current.onStateChange?.('speaking');\\n        \\n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\\n        utterance.pitch = 1;\\n        \\n        utterance.onend = () => {\\n            isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n            setState('idle');\\n            if (wasRunning) {\\n                shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n                setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 500);\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        utterance.onerror = () => {\\n            isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n            setState('idle');\\n        };\\n        \\n        synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n    }, [safeStart]);\\n    \\n    const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\\n        synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n        setState('idle');\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    return {\\n        state, transcript, interimTranscript, error,\\n        isListening: state === 'listening',\\n        isSpeaking: state === 'speaking',\\n        isProcessing: state === 'processing',\\n        isIdle: state === 'idle',\\n        isError: state === 'error',\\n        start, stop, toggle, speak, stopSpeaking, processVoiceInput\\n    };\\n}\\n\\nexport default useVoice;\\nVOICEHOOK\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Fixed Integration\\n */\\n\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\\nimport { useVoice } from '../hooks/useVoice';\\n\\ninterface WalkingCursorProps {\\n    enabled?: boolean;\\n    showVoice?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\nexport function WalkingCursor({ enabled = true, showVoice = true }: WalkingCursorProps) {\\n    const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x: 100, y: 100 });\\n    const isListening, toggle } = useVoice({\\n        userType: 'boss',\\n        onResponse: (data) => {\\n            console.log('[Walker] Got response:', data);\\n        }\\n    });\\n    \\n    // Follow mouse smoothly\\n    useEffect(() => {\\n        if (!enabled) return;\\n        \\n        const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {\\n            targetRef.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };\\n        };\\n        \\n        window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);\\n        \\n        const animate = () => {\\n            setPosition(prev => ({\\n                x: prev.x + (targetRef.current.x - prev.x) * 0.1,\\n                y: prev.y + (targetRef.current.y - prev.y) * 0.1\\n            }));\\n            animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n        };\\n        \\n        animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\\n        \\n        return () => {\\n            window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);\\n            if (animationRef.current) cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);\\n        };\\n    }, [enabled]);\\n    \\n    if (!enabled || !isVisible) return null;\\n    \\n    return (\\n        <div\\n            className=\\\"fixed pointer-events-none z-[9999] transition-opacity duration-300\\\"\\n            style={{\\n                left: position.x + 20,\\n                top: position.y + 20,\\n                transform: 'translate(0, 0)'\\n            }}\\n        >\\n            <div className={`\\n                flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-full\\n                ${isListening \\n                    ?   }\n    next();\n});\n\n// console.log('  \u2705 Database connected'))\n    .catch(err => console.error('  \u274c Database error:', err.message));\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// HELPER FUNCTIONS\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nfunction analyzeIntent(text) {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show|take me|redirect/)) return 'navigation';\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look for|where|what is|who is/)) return 'query';\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit|quit|end/)) return 'control';\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make|build/)) return 'create';\n    if (lower.match(/update|edit|change|modify/)) return 'update';\n    if (lower.match(/delete|remove|clear/)) return 'delete';\n    if (lower.match(/help|how do|explain|tell me/)) return 'help';\n    \n    return 'general';\n}\n\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    const positive = ['great', 'good', 'awesome', 'thanks', 'thank you', 'love', 'excellent', 'perfect', 'amazing', 'wonderful'];\n    const negative = ['bad', 'wrong', 'error', 'hate', 'terrible', 'awful', 'horrible', 'worst', 'sucks', 'broken'];\n    \n    for (const word of positive) {\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'positive';\n    }\n    for (const word of negative) {\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'negative';\n    }\n    \n    return 'neutral';\n}\n\nfunction analyzeEmotion(text) {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    if (lower.match(/happy|joy|excited|yay|woohoo/)) return 'happy';\n    if (lower.match(/sad|upset|disappointed|unfortunately/)) return 'sad';\n    if (lower.match(/angry|frustrated|annoyed|damn|ugh/)) return 'frustrated';\n    if (lower.match(/confused|lost|don't understand|what\\?/)) return 'confused';\n    if (lower.match(/worried|concerned|nervous/)) return 'worried';\n    \n    return 'neutral';\n}\n\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\n    const responses = {\n        navigation: {\n            positive: \"Absolutely! Taking you there right now!\",\n            negative: \"I'll navigate you there to help fix that.\",\n            neutral: \"Navigating there now, boss!\"\n        },\n        query: {\n            positive: \"Great question! Let me find that for you.\",\n            negative: \"Let me search for a solution.\",\n            neutral: \"Searching for that information...\"\n        },\n        control: {\n            positive: \"Done! Glad I could help!\",\n            negative: \"Stopped. Let me know what you need.\",\n            neutral: \"Action completed, boss!\"\n        },\n        create: {\n            positive: \"Awesome! Creating that now!\",\n            negative: \"I'll create that to help resolve this.\",\n            neutral: \"Creating that for you...\"\n        },\n        update: {\n            positive: \"Perfect! Updating now!\",\n            negative: \"Updating to fix that issue.\",\n            neutral: \"Making those changes...\"\n        },\n        delete: {\n            positive: \"Removed! All clean now.\",\n            negative: \"Deleted. Hope that helps.\",\n            neutral: \"Removed successfully.\"\n        },\n        help: {\n            positive: \"Happy to help! Here's what I know...\",\n            negative: \"Let me help you figure this out.\",\n            neutral: \"Here's how that works...\"\n        },\n        general: {\n            positive: \"Got it! I'm on it, boss!\",\n            negative: \"I understand. Let me help with that.\",\n            neutral: \"Understood. Processing your request...\"\n        }\n    };\n    \n    return responses[intent]?.[sentiment] || responses.general.neutral;\n}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// ENDPOINTS\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// Health check\napp.get('/api/health', (req, res) => {\n    res.json({ \n        status: 'ok', \n        version: '33.2',\n        timestamp: new Date().toISOString() \n    });\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// VOICE COMMAND - Main voice input endpoint\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\napp.post('/api/voice/command', async (req, res) => {\n    const { text, transcript, user_type = 'boss', page_route = '/' } = req.body;\n    const inputText = text || transcript;\n    \n    if (!inputText) {\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No text provided' });\n    }\n    \n    const startTime = Date.now();\n    \n    try {\n        // Analyze\n        const intent = analyzeIntent(inputText);\n        const sentiment = analyzeSentiment(inputText);\n        const emotion = analyzeEmotion(inputText);\n        const empathyScore = sentiment === 'positive' ? 0.9 : sentiment === 'negative' ? 0.6 : 0.75;\n        \n        // Save to global_interaction_ledger\n        const ledgerResult = await pool.query(`\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \n            (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathy_score, page_route, created_at)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, NOW())\n            RETURNING id\n        `, [user_type, inputText, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathyScore, page_route]);\n        \n        const ledgerId = ledgerResult.rows[0].id;\n        \n        // Save to boss_voice_inputs\n        try {\n            await pool.query(`\n                INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_transcript, intent, confidence, created_at)\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\n            `, [inputText, intent, 0.85]);\n        } catch (e) { /* table may not exist */ }\n        \n        // Learn pattern\n        try {\n            const patternText = inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100);\n            await pool.query(`\n                INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\n                VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW())\n                ON CONFLICT (pattern_text) \n                DO UPDATE SET \n                    occurrence_count = learned_patterns.occurrence_count + 1,\n                    last_seen = NOW()\n            `, [patternText, intent]);\n        } catch (e) { \n            // Try without conflict handling\n            try {\n                await pool.query(`\n                    INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\n                    VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW())\n                `, [inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100), intent]);\n            } catch (e2) { /* ignore */ }\n        }\n        \n        // Add to realtime feed\n        try {\n            await pool.query(`\n                INSERT INTO realtime_feed (event_type, event_data, source, created_at)\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\n            `, ['voice_command', JSON.stringify({ text: inputText, intent, sentiment }), user_type]);\n        } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n        \n        // Generate response\n        const responseText = generateResponse(intent, sentiment);\n        \n        // Log TTS response\n        try {\n            await pool.query(`\n                INSERT INTO tts_responses (input_text, response_text, tone, created_at)\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\n            `, [inputText, responseText, sentiment === 'positive' ? 'enthusiastic' : 'friendly']);\n        } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n        \n        const processingTime = Date.now() - startTime;\n        \n        console.log(`  [Voice] \"${inputText.substring(0, 40)}...\" \u2192 ${intent} (${processingTime}ms)`);\n        \n        res.json({\n            success: true,\n            ledger_id: ledgerId,\n            analysis: {\n                intent,\n                sentiment,\n                emotion,\n                empathyScore,\n                confidence: 0.85\n            },\n            response: {\n                text: responseText,\n                tone: sentiment === 'positive' ? 'enthusiastic' : 'friendly',\n                speak: true\n            },\n            processingTime\n        });\n        \n    } catch (err) {\n        console.error('  [Voice] Error:', err.message);\n        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });\n    }\n});\n\n// LEDGER LOG - Alternative/fallback endpoint\n// async (req, res) => {\n    const { user_type = 'boss', raw_transcript, page_route = '/' } = req.body;\n    \n    if (!raw_transcript) {\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No transcript provided' });\n    }\n    \n    try {\n        const intent = analyzeIntent(raw_transcript);\n        const sentiment = analyzeSentiment(raw_transcript);\n        const emotion = analyzeEmotion(raw_transcript);\n        const empathyScore = sentiment === 'positive' ? 0.9 : sentiment === 'negative' ? 0.6 : 0.75;\n        \n        const result = await pool.query(`\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \n            (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathy_score, page_route, created_at)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, NOW())\n            RETURNING id\n        `, [user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathyScore, page_route]);\n        \n        const responseText = generateResponse(intent, sentiment);\n        \n        console.log(`  [Ledger] \"${raw_transcript.substring(0, 40)}...\" \u2192 ${intent}`);\n        \n        res.json({\n            success: true,\n            ledger_id: result.rows[0].id,\n            analysis: {\n                sentiment,\n                emotion,\n                intent,\n                empathyScore\n            },\n            tts_response: {\n                text: responseText,\n                tone: 'friendly'\n            }\n        });\n        \n    } catch (err) {\n        console.error('  [Ledger] Error:', err.message);\n async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const queries = {\n            interactions: 'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM global_interaction_ledger',\n            patterns: 'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM      }\n        \n        // Calculate confidence based on data\n        const totalData = results.interactions + results.patterns + results.crawls;\n        const confidence = Math.min(0.5 + HELPER FUNCTIONS\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nfunction analyzeIntent(text) {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show|take me|redirect/)) return 'navigation';\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look for|where|what is|who is/)) return 'query';\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit|quit|end/)) return 'control';\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make|build/)) return 'create';\\n    if (lower.match(/update|edit|change|modify/)) return 'update';\\n    if (lower.match(/delete|remove|clear/)) return 'delete';\\n    if (lower.match(/help|how do|explain|tell me/)) return 'help';\\n    \\n    return 'general';\\n}\\n\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    const positive = ['great', 'good', 'awesome', 'thanks', 'thank you', 'love', 'excellent', 'perfect', 'amazing', 'wonderful'];\\n    const negative = ['bad', 'wrong', 'error', 'hate', 'terrible', 'awful', 'horrible', 'worst', 'sucks', 'broken'];\\n    \\n    for (const word of positive) {\\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'positive';\\n    }\\n    for (const word of negative) {\\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'negative';\\n    }\\n    \\n    return 'neutral';\\n}\\n\\nfunction analyzeEmotion(text) {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    if (lower.match(/happy|joy|excited|yay|woohoo/)) return 'happy';\\n    if (lower.match(/sad|upset|disappointed|unfortunately/)) return 'sad';\\n    if (lower.match(/angry|frustrated|annoyed|damn|ugh/)) return 'frustrated';\\n    if (lower.match(/confused|lost|don't understand|what\\\\?/)) return 'confused';\\n    if (lower.match(/worried|concerned|nervous/)) return 'worried';\\n    \\n    return 'neutral';\\n}\\n\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\n    const responses = {\\n        navigation: {\\n            positive: \\\"Absolutely! Taking you there right now!\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"I'll navigate you there to help fix that.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Navigating there now, boss!\\\"\\n        },\\n        query: {\\n            positive: \\\"Great question! Let me find that for you.\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"Let me search for a solution.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Searching for that information...\\\"\\n        },\\n        control: {\\n            positive: \\\"Done! Glad I could help!\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"Stopped. Let me know what you need.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Action completed, boss!\\\"\\n        },\\n        create: {\\n            positive: \\\"Awesome! Creating that now!\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"I'll create that to help resolve this.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Creating that for you...\\\"\\n        },\\n        update: {\\n            positive: \\\"Perfect! Updating now!\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"Updating to fix that issue.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Making those changes...\\\"\\n        },\\n        delete: {\\n            positive: \\\"Removed! All clean now.\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"Deleted. Hope that helps.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Removed successfully.\\\"\\n        },\\n        help: {\\n            positive: \\\"Happy to help! Here's what I know...\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"Let me help you figure this out.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Here's how that works...\\\"\\n        },\\n        general: {\\n            positive: \\\"Got it! I'm on it, boss!\\\",\\n            negative: \\\"I understand. Let me help with that.\\\",\\n            neutral: \\\"Understood. Processing your request...\\\"\\n        }\\n    };\\n    \\n    return responses[intent]?.[sentiment] || responses.general.neutral;\\n}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// `, [patternText, intent]);\\n        } catch (e) { \\n            // Try without conflict handling\\n            try {\\n                await pool.query(`\\n                    INSERT INTO voiceHandler = async (req, res) => {\n    const { text, transcript, user_type = 'boss', page_route = '/' } = req.body;\n    const inputText = text || transcript;\n    if (!inputText) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No text' });\n    \n    try {\n        const intent = analyzeIntent(inputText);\n        const sentiment = analyzeSentiment(inputText);\n        \n        const result = await pool.query(`\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, page_route, created_at)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, NOW()) RETURNING id\n        `, [user_type, inputText, intent, sentiment, page_route]);\n        \n        try { await pool.query(`INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_transcript, intent, confidence, created_at) VALUES ($1, $2, 0.85, NOW())`, [inputText, intent]); } catch {}\n        try { await pool.query(`INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen) VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW()) ON CONFLICT (pattern_text) DO UPDATE SET occurrence_count = learned_patterns.occurrence_count + 1, last_seen = NOW()`, [inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0,100), intent]); } catch {}\n        try { await pool.query(`INSERT INTO realtime_feed (event_type, event_data, source, created_at) VALUES ('voice', $1, $2, NOW())`, [JSON.stringify({text: inputText, intent}), user_type]); } catch {}\n        \n        console.log(`[Voice] \"${inputText.substring(0,30)}...\" \u2192 ${intent}`);\n        res.json({ success: true, ledger_id: result.rows[0].id, analysis: { intent, sentiment }, response: $3, $4, $5, NOW()) RETURNING id`, [user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, page_route]);\n        res.json({ success: true, ledger_id: result.rows[0].id, analysis: { intent, sentiment }, { c[t] = 0; }\n        }\n        res.json({ interactions: c.global_interaction_ledger, patterns: c.learned_patterns, webCrawls: c.crawled_sources, voiceCommands: c.boss_voice_inputs, confidence: }\n};\napp.get('/ai/training/stats', statsHandler);\napp.get('/api/ai/training/stats', statsHandler);\n\n// Dashboard JSON\nconst dashboardHandler = async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const c =
